<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-align: center;"><i><b>Full-Year Operating Cash Flow ($5) million vs. ($12.8) million prior year&nbsp;</b></i></p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-align: center;"><i><b>Year ending cash balance of $21.7M&nbsp;</b></i></p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#8220;Reflecting on solid Q4 results, iCAD has demonstrated strong execution and progress towards our three-phased transformation plan - realigning our base, strengthening our foundation, and investing in growth initiatives &#8211; allowing us to drive towards our patient-centric mission of creating a world where cancer can&#8217;t hide,&#8221; said Dana Brown, President and CEO, iCAD. In the last five years alone, iCAD estimates reading more than 40 million mammograms worldwide, of which nearly 30% are tomosynthesis.&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Total revenue for the&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="45x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F20233211682094135047">fourth</a> quarter of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="5" id="led395579F20233211682094146687">2023</a> was $4.7&nbsp;million, an increase of $0.1&nbsp;million, or 2%, as compared to the <a data-tblloc="45x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F20233211682094135047">fourth</a> quarter of <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="5" id="led395579F20233211682094193775">2022</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Operating Expenses: Total operating expenses for the <a data-tblloc="45x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F20233211682094135047">fourth</a> quarter of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="5" id="led395579F20233211682094146687">2023</a> were $5.0&nbsp;million, a 22% decrease from $6.5&nbsp;million in the <a data-tblloc="45x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F20233211682094135047">fourth</a> quarter of <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="5" id="led395579F20233211682094193775">2022</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Gross Profit: Gross profit for the <a data-tblloc="49x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F202310201700497131732">twelve</a>&nbsp;months ended <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F202310201700496799468">December 31, 2023</a> was $14.8&nbsp;million, or 85% of revenue, as compared to $16.8&nbsp;million, or 85% of revenue, for&nbsp;the <a data-tblloc="49x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F202310201700497131732">twelve</a>&nbsp;months ended <a data-tblloc="9x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F202310201700497247631">December 31, 2022</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Operating Expenses: Total operating expenses for the <a data-tblloc="49x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F202310201700497131732">twelve</a> months ended <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F202310201700496799468">December 31, 2023</a> were $22.5&nbsp;million, a 17% decrease from $27.0&nbsp;million for the <a data-tblloc="49x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F202310201700497131732">twelve</a>&nbsp;months ended <a data-tblloc="9x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F202310201700497247631">December 31, 2022</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">GAAP Net Loss from continuing operations: Net loss from continuing operations for the <a data-tblloc="49x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F202310201700497131732">twelve</a> months ended <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F202310201700496799468">December 31, 2023</a> was ($7.0) million, or ($0.27)&nbsp;per diluted share, as compared to a net loss of ($9.9) million, or ($0.39) per diluted share, for the <a data-tblloc="49x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F202310201700497131732">twelve</a>&nbsp;months ended <a data-tblloc="9x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F202310201700497247631">December 31, 2022</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Non-GAAP Adjusted Net Loss from continuing operations: Non-GAAP Adjusted Net Loss from continuing operations, a non-GAAP financial measure as defined below, for the <a data-tblloc="49x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F202310201700497131732">twelve</a> months ended <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F202310201700496799468">December 31, 2023</a> was ($6.8) million, or ($0.27) per diluted share, as compared to a Non-GAAP Adjusted Net Loss of ($9.8) million, or ($0.39) per diluted share, for the <a data-tblloc="49x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F202310201700497131732">twelve</a> months ended <a data-tblloc="9x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F202310201700497247631">December 31, 2022</a>.&nbsp; Please refer to the section entitled &#8220;Reconciliation of Non-GAAP Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP Measures&#8221; and the accompanying financial table included at the end of this release for a reconciliation of GAAP Net Loss to Non-GAAP Adjusted Net Loss results for the <a data-tblloc="49x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F202310201700497131732">twelve</a>-month periods ended <a data-tblloc="7x1" data-tblname="395579" data-tblv="5" id="led395579F20233211682094343599">December 31, 2023 and 2022</a>, respectively.</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Cash and cash equivalents:&#8239; Cash&nbsp;and cash equivalents were $21.7&nbsp;million as of <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="395578" data-tblv="5" id="led395578F202310201700496799468">December 31, 2023</a>. During the year ended December 31, 2023, the Company generated net proceeds of approximately $2.0&nbsp;million from the issuance of 1,057,814&nbsp;shares of common stock in at-the-market (ATM) offerings at a weighted average price of $2.18&nbsp;per share.&nbsp; In addition, the Xoft sale in October 2023 resulted in net cash proceeds of $4.5&nbsp;million.&nbsp; Accordingly, iCAD believes it has sufficient cash resources to fund its planned operations with no need to raise additional funding.&#8239;</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;"><b>Use of Non-GAAP Financial Measures </b></p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">In its quarterly news releases, conference calls, slide presentations or webcasts, the Company may use or discuss non-GAAP financial measures as defined by SEC Regulation G. The GAAP financial measures most directly comparable to each non-GAAP financial measure used or discussed, and a reconciliation of the differences between each non-GAAP financial measure and the comparable GAAP financial measure, are included in this press release after the condensed consolidated financial statements. When analyzing the Company&#8217;s operating performance, investors should not consider these non-GAAP measures as a substitute for the comparable financial measures prepared in accordance with GAAP. The Company&#8217;s quarterly news releases containing such non-GAAP reconciliations can be found on the Investors section of the Company&#8217;s website at www.icadmed.com.</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b>About iCAD, Inc. </b></p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Headquartered in Nashua, NH, iCAD is a global medical technology leader providing innovative cancer detection and therapy solutions. For more information, visit&nbsp;<u>www.icadmed.com.</u></p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;"><b>Forward-Looking Statements&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</b></p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;"><b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</b></p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">Certain statements contained in this News Release constitute &#8220;forward-looking statements&#8221; within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995, including statements about the expansion of access to the Company&#8217;s products, improvement of performance, acceleration of adoption, expected benefits of ProFound AI&#174;, the benefits of the Company&#8217;s products, and future prospects for the Company&#8217;s technology platforms and products. Such forward-looking statements involve a number of known and unknown risks, uncertainties and other factors which may cause the actual results, performance, or achievements of the Company to be materially different from any future results, performance, or achievements expressed or implied by such forward-looking statements. Such factors include, but are not limited, to the Company&#8217;s ability to achieve business and strategic objectives, the willingness of patients to undergo mammography screening in light of risks of potential exposure to Covid-19, whether mammography screening will be treated as an essential procedure, whether ProFound AI will improve reading efficiency, improve specificity and sensitivity, reduce false positives and otherwise prove to be more beneficial for patients and clinicians, the impact of supply and manufacturing constraints or difficulties on our ability to fulfill our orders, uncertainty of future sales levels, to defend itself in litigation matters, protection of patents and other proprietary rights, product market acceptance, possible technological obsolescence of products, increased competition, government regulation, changes in Medicare or other reimbursement policies, risks relating to our existing and future debt obligations, competitive factors, the effects of a decline in the economy or markets served by the Company; and other risks detailed in the Company&#8217;s filings with the Securities and Exchange Commission. The words &#8220;believe,&#8221; &#8220;demonstrate,&#8221; &#8220;intend,&#8221; &#8220;expect,&#8221; &#8220;estimate,&#8221; &#8220;will,&#8221; &#8220;continue,&#8221; &#8220;anticipate,&#8221; &#8220;likely,&#8221; &#8220;seek,&#8221; and similar expressions identify forward-looking statements. The Company is under no obligation to provide any updates to any information contained in this release. For additional disclosure regarding these and other risks faced by iCAD, please see the disclosure contained in our public filings with the Securities and Exchange Commission, available on the Investors section of our website at http://www.icadmed.com and on the SEC&#8217;s website at http://www.sec.gov.&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b>Reconciliation of Non-GAAP Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP Measures and Definitions</b></p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The Company reports its financial results in accordance with United States generally accepted accounting principles, or GAAP. However, management believes that in order to understand the Company&#8217;s short-term and long-term financial and operational trends, investors may wish to consider the impact of certain non-cash or non-recurring items, when used as a supplement to financial performance measures in accordance with GAAP. These items result from facts and circumstances that vary in frequency and/or impact on continuing operations. Management also uses results of operations before such items to evaluate the operating performance of the Company and compare it against past periods, make operating decisions, and serve as a basis for strategic planning. These non-GAAP financial measures provide management with additional means to understand and evaluate the operating results and trends in the Company&#8217;s ongoing business by eliminating certain non-cash expenses and other items that management believes might otherwise make comparisons of the Company&#8217;s ongoing business with prior periods more difficult, obscure trends in ongoing operations or reduce management&#8217;s ability to make useful forecasts. Management believes that these non-GAAP financial measures provide additional means of evaluating period-over-period operating performance. In addition, management understands that some investors and financial analysts find this information helpful in analyzing the Company&#8217;s financial and operational performance and comparing this performance to its peers and competitors.</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Management defines &#8220;Non-GAAP Adjusted EBITDA&#8221; as the sum of GAAP Net Loss before provisions for interest expense, other income, stock-based compensation expense, depreciation and amortization, tax expense, severance, gain on sale of assets, loss on disposal of assets, acquisition and litigation related expenses. Management considers this non-GAAP financial measure to be an indicator of the Company&#8217;s operational strength and performance of its business and a good measure of its historical operating trends, in particular the extent to which ongoing operations impact the Company&#8217;s overall financial performance.</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The non-GAAP financial measures do not replace the presentation of the Company&#8217;s GAAP financial results and should only be used as a supplement to, not as a substitute for, the Company&#8217;s financial results presented in accordance with GAAP. The Company has provided a reconciliation of each non-GAAP financial measure used in its financial reporting and investor presentations to the most directly comparable GAAP financial measure.</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Management excludes each of the items identified below from the applicable non-GAAP financial measure referenced above for the reasons set forth with respect to that excluded item:</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 27pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#8226;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Interest expense: The Company excludes interest expense which includes interest from the facility agreement, interest on capital leases and interest on the convertible debentures from its non-GAAP Adjusted EBITDA calculation.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

		<tr style="vertical-align: top; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 27pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#8226;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Stock-based compensation expense: excluded as these are non-cash expenses that management does not consider part of ongoing operating results when assessing the performance of the Company&#8217;s business, and also because the total amount of expense is partially outside of the Company&#8217;s control as it is based on factors such as stock price volatility and interest rates, which may be unrelated to our performance during the period in which the expense is incurred.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

		<tr style="vertical-align: top; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 27pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#8226;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Amortization and Depreciation: Purchased assets and intangibles are amortized over a period of several years and generally cannot be changed or influenced by management after they are acquired. Accordingly, these non-cash items are not considered by management in making operating decisions, and management believes that such expenses do not have a direct correlation to future business operations. Thus, including such charges does not accurately reflect the performance of the Company&#8217;s ongoing operations for the period in which such charges are incurred.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

		<tr style="vertical-align: top; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 27pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>

			</td>
			<td style="width: auto; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Severance and Furlough: The Company has incurred severance and furlough expenses in connection with restructuring and in connection with the separation of its former CEO.&nbsp; The Company excludes these items from its non-GAAP financial measures when evaluating its continuing business performance as such&nbsp;items can vary significantly and do not reflect expected future operating expenses. In addition, management believes that such items do not have a direct correlation to future business operations.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

		<tr style="vertical-align: top; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 27pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>

			</td>
			<td style="width: auto; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Loss on fair value of convertible debentures. The Company excludes this non-cash item as it is not considered by management in making operating decisions, and management believes that such item does not have a direct correlation to future business operations.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 27pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#8226;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Litigation related: These expenses consist primarily of settlement, legal and other professional fees related to litigation. The Company excludes these costs from its non-GAAP measures primarily because the Company believes that these costs have no direct correlation to the core operations of the Company.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 27pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#8226;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Loss on extinguishment of debt: The Company excludes this non-cash item as it is not considered by management in making operating decisions, and management believes that such item does not have a direct correlation to future business operations.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">On occasion in the future, there may be other items, such as loss on extinguishment of debt, significant asset impairments, restructuring charges or significant gains or losses from contingencies that the Company may exclude if it believes that doing so is consistent with the goal of providing useful information to investors and management.</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;"><b><u>Definitions</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">Starting in the third quarter of 2023, the Company began reporting Annual Recurring Revenue (&#8220;ARR&#8221;) with each quarterly earnings announcement.&nbsp; The Company&#8217;s management believes this is a useful metric for purposes of assessing progress in transitioning to a subscription-based business model.&nbsp; ARR should be viewed independently of revenue and does not represent our revenue under U.S. GAAP on an annualized basis, as it is an operating metric that can be impacted by contract start dates, end dates, cancellations, and renewal rates. Subscription ARR is not intended to be a replacement for forecasts of revenue. &nbsp;The following are the variations of ARR the Company intends to present:</p>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 37pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">1.</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Total ARR (T-ARR) represents the annualized value of subscription license, maintenance contracts and active cloud services at the end of a reporting period.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 37pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">2.</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Maintenance Services ARR (M-ARR) represents the annualized value of active perpetual license maintenance service contracts at the end of the reporting period.&nbsp;</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 37pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">3.</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Subscription ARR (S-ARR) represents the annualized value of active subscription or term licenses at the end of a reporting period.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 37pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">4.</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Cloud ARR (C-ARR) represents the annualized value of active cloud services contracts at the end of a reporting period.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: Calibri, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>
